       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <p>Yale has produced alumni distinguished in their respective fields. Among the best-known are U.S.&nbsp;Presidents <a href="/wiki/William_Howard_Taft" title="William Howard Taft">William Howard Taft</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gerald_Ford" title="Gerald Ford">Gerald Ford</a>, <a href="/wiki/George_H._W._Bush" title="George H. W. Bush">George H.&nbsp;W. Bush</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bill_Clinton" title="Bill Clinton">Bill Clinton</a> and <a href="/wiki/George_W._Bush" title="George W. Bush">George W. Bush</a>; Royals <a href="/wiki/Prince_Rostislav_Romanov_(born_1985)" title="Prince Rostislav Romanov (born 1985)">Prince Rostislav Romanov</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kyebambe_III_of_Toro" title="Kyebambe III of Toro">Prince Akiiki Hosea Nyabongo</a>; Italian Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Mario_Monti" title="Mario Monti">Mario Monti</a>; Supreme Court Justices <a href="/wiki/Sonia_Sotomayor" title="Sonia Sotomayor">Sonia Sotomayor</a>, <a href="/wiki/Samuel_Alito" title="Samuel Alito">Samuel Alito</a> and <a href="/wiki/Clarence_Thomas" title="Clarence Thomas">Clarence Thomas</a>; U.S.&nbsp; Secretaries of State <a href="/wiki/John_Kerry" title="John Kerry">John Kerry</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hillary_Rodham_Clinton" title="Hillary Rodham Clinton">Hillary Rodham Clinton</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cyrus_Vance" title="Cyrus Vance">Cyrus Vance</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Dean_Acheson" title="Dean Acheson">Dean Acheson</a>; authors <a href="/wiki/Sinclair_Lewis" title="Sinclair Lewis">Sinclair Lewis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Stephen_Vincent_Ben%C3%A9t" title="Stephen Vincent Ben&eacute;t">Stephen Vincent Ben&eacute;t</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Tom_Wolfe" title="Tom Wolfe">Tom Wolfe</a>; lexicographer <a href="/wiki/Noah_Webster" title="Noah Webster">Noah Webster</a>; inventors <a href="/wiki/Samuel_F._B._Morse" title="Samuel F. B. Morse" class="mw-redirect">Samuel F.&nbsp;B. Morse</a> and <a href="/wiki/Eli_Whitney" title="Eli Whitney">Eli Whitney</a>; patriot and &quot;first spy&quot; <a href="/wiki/Nathan_Hale" title="Nathan Hale">Nathan Hale</a>; theologian <a href="/wiki/Jonathan_Edwards_(theologian)" title="Jonathan Edwards (theologian)">Jonathan Edwards</a>; actors, directors and producers <a href="/wiki/Paul_Newman" title="Paul Newman">Paul Newman</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Price" title="Vincent Price">Vincent Price</a>, <a href="/wiki/Meryl_Streep" title="Meryl Streep">Meryl Streep</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jodie_Foster" title="Jodie Foster">Jodie Foster</a>, <a href="/wiki/Angela_Bassett" title="Angela Bassett">Angela Bassett</a>, <a href="/wiki/Courtney_Vance" title="Courtney Vance" class="mw-redirect">Courtney Vance</a>, <a href="/wiki/Frances_McDormand" title="Frances McDormand">Frances McDormand</a>, <a href="/wiki/Elia_Kazan" title="Elia Kazan">Elia Kazan</a>, <a href="/wiki/George_Roy_Hill" title="George Roy Hill">George Roy Hill</a>, <a href="/wiki/Oliver_Stone" title="Oliver Stone">Oliver Stone</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sam_Waterson" title="Sam Waterson" class="mw-redirect">Sam Waterson</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Michael_Cimino" title="Michael Cimino">Michael Cimino</a>; &quot;Father of American football&quot; <a href="/wiki/Walter_Camp" title="Walter Camp">Walter Camp</a>, &quot;The perfect oarsman&quot; <a href="/wiki/Rusty_Wailes" title="Rusty Wailes">Rusty Wailes</a>; composers <a href="/wiki/Charles_Ives" title="Charles Ives">Charles Ives</a>, <a href="/wiki/Douglas_Moore" title="Douglas Moore">Douglas Moore</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cole_Porter" title="Cole Porter">Cole Porter</a>; Peace Corps founder <a href="/wiki/Sargent_Shriver" title="Sargent Shriver">Sargent Shriver</a>; child psychologist <a href="/wiki/Benjamin_Spock" title="Benjamin Spock">Benjamin Spock</a>; sculptor <a href="/wiki/Richard_Serra" title="Richard Serra">Richard Serra</a>; film critic <a href="/wiki/Gene_Siskel" title="Gene Siskel">Gene Siskel</a>; television commentators <a href="/wiki/Dick_Cavett" title="Dick Cavett">Dick Cavett</a> and <a href="/wiki/Anderson_Cooper" title="Anderson Cooper">Anderson Cooper</a>; <a href="/wiki/Pundit_(expert)" title="Pundit (expert)" class="mw-redirect">pundits</a> <a href="/wiki/William_F._Buckley,_Jr." title="William F. Buckley, Jr.">William F. Buckley,&nbsp;Jr.</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Fareed_Zakaria" title="Fareed Zakaria">Fareed Zakaria</a>; <a href="/wiki/Time_Magazine" title="Time Magazine" class="mw-redirect">Time Magazine</a> co-founder <a href="/wiki/Henry_Luce" title="Henry Luce">Henry Luce</a>; President of Mexico <a href="/wiki/Ernesto_Zedillo" title="Ernesto Zedillo">Ernesto Zedillo</a>; President of the Federal Republic of Germany <a href="/wiki/Karl_Carstens" title="Karl Carstens">Karl Carstens</a>; Philippines President <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Paciano_Laurel" title="Jos&eacute; Paciano Laurel" class="mw-redirect">Jos&eacute; Paciano Laurel</a>; Nobel Laureate in Economics and popular book author <a href="/wiki/Paul_Krugman" title="Paul Krugman">Paul Krugman</a>; inventor of the <a href="/wiki/Cyclotron" title="Cyclotron">cyclotron</a> and Nobel Laureate in Physics, <a href="/wiki/Ernest_Lawrence" title="Ernest Lawrence">Ernest Lawrence</a>; director of the <a href="/wiki/Human_Genome_Project" title="Human Genome Project">Human Genome Project</a>, <a href="/wiki/Francis_S._Collins" title="Francis S. Collins" class="mw-redirect">Francis S. Collins</a>; economist <a href="/wiki/Irving_Fischer" title="Irving Fischer" class="mw-redirect">Irving Fischer</a>, &quot;The Father of Monetarism&quot;; mathematician and chemist <a href="/wiki/Josiah_Willard_Gibbs" title="Josiah Willard Gibbs">Josiah Willard Gibbs</a>; <a href="/wiki/Morgan_Stanley" title="Morgan Stanley">Morgan Stanley</a> founder <a href="/wiki/Harold_Stanley" title="Harold Stanley">Harold Stanley</a>; <a href="/wiki/Boeing" title="Boeing">Boeing</a> CEO <a href="/wiki/James_McNerney" title="James McNerney">James McNerney</a>; <a href="/wiki/FedEx" title="FedEx">FedEx</a> founder <a href="/wiki/Frederick_W._Smith" title="Frederick W. Smith">Frederick W. Smith</a>; Turkish prime minister <a href="/wiki/Tansu_%C3%87iller" title="Tansu &Ccedil;iller">Tansu &Ccedil;iller</a>; <a href="/wiki/Time_Warner" title="Time Warner">Time Warner</a> president <a href="/wiki/Jeffrey_Bewkes" title="Jeffrey Bewkes">Jeffrey Bewkes</a>; Electronic Arts co-founder <a href="/wiki/Bing_Gordon" title="Bing Gordon">Bing Gordon</a>; architects <a href="/wiki/Eero_Saarinen" title="Eero Saarinen">Eero Saarinen</a> and <a href="/wiki/Norman_Foster" title="Norman Foster" class="mw-redirect">Norman Foster</a>.</p> 
     <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Yale_in_fiction_and_popular_culture">Yale in fiction and popular culture</span><span class="mw-editsection">[<a href="/w/index.php?title=Yale_University&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Yale in fiction and popular culture">edit</a>]</span></h2> 
     <div class="rellink">
      Further information: 
      <a href="/wiki/List_of_Yale_University_people" title="List of Yale University people">List of Yale University people</a>&nbsp;and&nbsp;
      <a href="/wiki/Yale_in_popular_culture" title="Yale in popular culture">Yale in popular culture</a>
     </div> 
     <p>Yale University, one of the oldest universities in the United States, is a <a href="/wiki/Culture" title="Culture">cultural referent</a> as an institution that produces some of the most elite members of society<sup id="cite_ref-isbn0-8014-3479-3_145-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-isbn0-8014-3479-3-145"><span>[</span>145<span>]</span></a></sup> and its grounds, alumni, and students have been prominently portrayed in fiction and U.S. popular culture. For example, <a href="/wiki/Owen_Johnson_(writer)" title="Owen Johnson (writer)">Owen Johnson</a>'s novel, <i>Stover at Yale</i>, follows the college career of Dink Stover<sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146"><span>[</span>146<span>]</span></a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Frank_Merriwell" title="Frank Merriwell">Frank Merriwell</a>, the model for all later juvenile sports fiction, plays football, baseball, crew, and track at Yale while solving mysteries and righting wrongs.<sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147"><span>[</span>147<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148"><span>[</span>148<span>]</span></a></sup> Yale University was also mentioned in <a href="/wiki/F._Scott_Fitzgerald" title="F. Scott Fitzgerald">F. Scott Fitzgerald</a>'s novel &quot;<a href="/wiki/The_Great_Gatsby" title="The Great Gatsby">The Great Gatsby</a>&quot;. Nick Carraway and Tom Buchanan have both graduated from New Haven. The narrator (the former) has written a series of editorials for the <i>Yale News</i> and the following has been &quot;one of the most powerful <a href="/wiki/Defensive_end" title="Defensive end">ends</a> that ever played football at New Haven&quot;.</p>
